< Text>
Would NOT RECOMMEND!!

Recently moved here from Florida and was in search for a good dental practice geared towards kids

They had great google reviews ( now wondering how many are staff or staff family & friends written ) so I chose here .

BIG MISTAKE!!

If you have children under 7 don't waste your time !!
It's a CHILDREN dental group that charge 125 $ EXTRA if you have a child they consider " fidgety " or needs " a little more time to prep " and a 45$ for oral sedation ( currently studying and you should be warned small kidneys and livers should NOT take this ) they will say it's optional but FORCE it on you !

I had to speak with a manager after my appointment to be refunded the " optional oral sedation 45$ and behavior management fee of 125$ " after explaining they did NOTHING special in time nor did my child have the oral sedation drink smh what a headache!!

Be warned stay away with smaller children !!
A kids dental group that charges EXTRA to deal with children .. smh...

THE IRONY OF THAT!

Yes it's pretty everything that looks nice is not.< /Text>

<user>108495031304909731512< /user><name>Jen Hoffman<//name><Time>1556142435446< /Time><Rating>2<//Rating>< text>
I'm hoping this review may be helpful to parents looking for a new pediatric dentist. We recently moved here, made an appt for end of April. Took about 3.5 weeks to get an appt, which I find to be average for busy pediatric dentists. Staff was very nice and professional. We arrive 20 minutes early to fill out paperwork. Waiting area has TV and a really neat fish tank for kids, but not much else. Waiting room filled up VERY fast to where there was no room to sit and patients were going out into the foyer area to wait. We kept waiting and waiting. Watching all the other people come in after us get called was slightly frustrating without an acknowledgment about how long we were waiting. Another new patient there for a consult said they had been waiting over an hour. After about 40 min, I pick up my cranky un-napped 2 year old and tell the lady that I'm going to have to reschedule. Just then (of course) we get our name called. We walk back and there is ANOTHER waiting room that is packed with kids and parents, nowhere to sit. My 2 year old is off the chain by this point, trying to run everywhere, screaming, no one there to acknowledge how long we all had been waiting. We waited for another 15 min or so. I quickly saw this was going to keep going on. After an hour of being there I scoop up my 2 year old and tell them thanks, but I was leaving and I needed to reschedule. Not a good first impression. I also want to add they do not offer silver diamine fluoride or SDF for young children with cavities that prevents further decay without doing a filling. It's probably one of the greatest things since sliced bread. It prevented my 2 year old from having to deal with sedation. The dentist just paints in on the cavity area every 6 months and off he goes! Why they don't offer this service is beyond me. I wouldn't want to do a filling on a 2 year old.  I hope this office will consider it one day. For now, we found an AWESOME pediatric dentist that does it in Visalia. Got us in for an appt same day and had no wait. I definitely don't expect that quick of service, but waiting an hour to be seen is subpar.<//text>

The food is great quality here, and for very cheap. There's a few drawbacks though. First is that you have to order chips separately from you order, instead of it being included with most items like many other Mexican restaurants do. The second drawback is that the inside is very small and cramped and can be dirty and loud at times. Because of that, I would recommend coming here for takeout only and taking it to a park or the beach and enjoying it there.</Text>

< Review>
This is a great cantina, very authentic Mexican food. You can tell any weekday from 11:30 to 1:00 by the line of Hispanic workers out the door. I went there almost every day when working nearby and had to stop eating the burritos because I was gaining weight.  I estimate each burrito is over a pound and delicious. Choose from Carnitas, Pollo, Carne Asada, Pesca or they even have Breakfast burritos with 2 eggs. Black or refried frijoles. Really hot salsas and other treats on the side board. And this is only the burritos.  They have enchiladas, Chile Relleno, tostadas, tacos and more. They also supply take away for parties, and they take phone orders.  I love my Cousins, but I don't go there too much any more, I don't want to be the Gordo Viejo!!!< /Review>

< Review>
Nice shop, wide variety. Most impressed by trade in value. I took a handful of records to another local shop and was offered $15 in cash, $18 in trade value, which seemed super low. I then brought the same records here and was offered $45 cash and $60 in trade value. This shop offers the best value for trading in records in at least the South Bay area. I'll be back!<//Review>

<rate>5< /rate><review>There is no place in Visalia to get better fried rice. One of these days I will find out your secrets Lao Noodle House!! One thing I love about this establishment is their sizes. They have a variety of sizes for every dish, from small to either extra-large or extra-extra-large (I can't quite remember)
Let me tell you, an extra-large fried rice will last you a couple days, and it's just as good reheated! You can also get amazing soup or pad Thai here, depending on whatever your craving. Don't forget to add on a Thai iced tea and some chicken and rice to make the perfect meal.
The staff is so friendly and interactive- the owner and his son are really fun to chat with!
Keep in mind they only accept cash payment. As of right now, it's only take-out due to COVID, so they'll remind you on the phone that it's cash only. Honestly not a big deal for me personally but it is a good thing to remember.
For the three years I've lived in the area, Lao Noodle House has been a regular visit for me, and that's not going to change any time soon!</review>< gmap_id>

< Text>
I wanted to share the experience I just had with Memorial Care Imaging, both the Newport Beach and Huntington Beach offices. I was scheduled this morning for an ultrasound at 8:30am, and unfortunately I received a call from a representative at the Newport Beach office that their ultrasound machine was not working. Instead of just scheduling me for the next time that their machine would be functioning, the representative, whom I apologize for not remembering her name, made the effort to reschedule me for just under (3) hours later at the Huntington Beach office. Upon arrival, I was immediately greeted by a young man who checked me in (again, I apologize for not remembering his name). He was very professional, attentive, and helped make me feel comfortable. He was not only that way with me, but also with other patients who checked in thereafter. Nicole, the technician who conducted the ultrasound, was just wonderful. She was also very professional, attentive to my concerns, and very trusting from the moment she called me and took me back to the examination room. I just left their office, and I will say that this was one of the best experiences I have ever had. Thanks to everyone at both the Newport Beach and Huntington Beach offices for making patients like myself feel comfortable.<//Text>

<name>Tracie Hall< /name>< Text>
Reception area comfortable and provides water and maybe coffee. I didn't visit the table and don't recall. Receptionists are friendly. My MRI technician was friendly, I got to wear my own clothes (stretch pants and sweatshirt) because clearly had no metal in them and removed my glasses. I'd come prepared for no metal with no jewelry (or any metal clasped underthings) so after leaving purse in locker could go straight to MRI room. My tech, Asia, was super helpful in alleviating the anxiety about a possible claustrophobic attack, explaining that you go in feet first, get earplugs AND a headset that plays lovely music, AND a squeezy bulb to cling to if you need her.  She warned the machine makes hideous loud noises.  I closed my eyes til close to the end when I opened just one and wished I hadn't for how tight the space was but I was able to stay calm for the few minutes left...15 total for my left side sciatica symptoms.  Was so pleased to come out alive and, even better, without having made a fool of myself!  They handed me a CD of the scan and let me know the Dr. would receive the report within 3 days.  I think that it's because I mentioned, in passing, that I would be seeing her later that afternoon, that they were able, and kind enough, to get it to her before I got to her office 6 hours later.< /Text>
